SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[CategoryId], [p0].[CompanyId], [p0].[CreationTime], [p0].[Description], [p0].[ExpirationTime], [p0].[ImageUrl], [p0].[Name], [p0].[Price], [p0].[Quantity], [p0].[Status], [u0].[Id], [u0].[Email], [u0].[Password], [u0].[Role], [u0].[UserName], [u0].[Balance], [u0].[ImageUrl], [u0].[IsActivated], [c].[Id], [c].[Name]
FROM (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CompanyId], [p].[CreationTime], [p].[Description], [p].[ExpirationTime], [p].[ImageUrl], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Quantity], [p].[Status]
    FROM [ProductOffers] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[Status] = 0
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [p0]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [u].[Id], [u].[Email], [u].[Password], [u].[Role], [u].[UserName], [u].[Balance], [u].[ImageUrl], [u].[IsActivated]
    FROM [Users] AS [u]
    WHERE [u].[Role] = 1
